-04- COMMANDS
------------------------------------------------------------

?-Nuke
-------
??? times, use a random non-elemental magic damage skill.
Equal chance of any of the following:
  7-Flush, Bahamut, Blow Fish, Bum Rush, Chocobop, Cokatrice, Crusader, Drain, Flare, Flash, GrandTrain, H-Bomb, HyperDrive, L.4 Flare, Land Slide, Maduin, Megahit, Meteo, Meteor, Osmose, Quasar, Rage, Raid, Rasp, Retort, Shock Wave, Shrapnel, Stunner, TekMissile, Ultima, Whump, Wombat

BioBlas
-------
Use the skill 'Bio Blaster'

CarbMan
-------
Use the combo Carbunkl + Mantra.

MegaVol
-------
Use the skill 'Mega Volt'

R-Bless
-------
Use a random ally beneficial-status skill.

  (3/32 chance each)  Big Guard
  (2/32 chance each)  Antdot
  (1/32 chance each)  Bserk, Carbunkl, Fenrir, Float, ForceField, Golem, Harvester, Haste, Haste2, Kirin, Kitty, Life 3, Palidor, Phantom, Quick, Regen, Remedy, Rflect, Safe, Shell, Tapir, TekBarrier, Unicorn, Vanish, WallChange, Warp, ZoneSeek

R-Geo
-------
Use a random geomancer-type Dance move.
Equal chance of any of the following:
  Antlion, Cave In, El Nino, Elf Fire, Harvester, Land Slide, Plasma, Rage, Sand Storm, Snare, Snowball, Sonic Boom, Specter, Sun Bath, Surge, Wind Slash

R-White
-------
Use a random white magic spell.

  (4/16 chance each)  Regen
  (3/16 chance each)  Life 2
  (2/16 chance each)  Cure 2, Life 3
  (1/16 chance each)  Antdot, Cure, Cure 3, Life, Remedy

Ragnaro
-------
Use the skill 'Ragnarok'

RaidCon
-------
Use the combo Raid + Confusion.

W-Demi
-------
2 times, use the skill 'Demi'
